    Saṅ Hyaṅ Hayu

    edited by Aditia Gunawan

    Filename: DHARMA_DiplEdSangHyangHayuPerpusnasL634.xml

    Language: Old Javanese

    Repository: Nusantara Philology (tfd-nusantara-philology)

    Version: part commented based on limited calls

    Witness

    • Jakarta, Perpustakaan Nasional Republik Indonesia, Lontar, L. 634
      • Content:
        • Vipañcitārthā by Śāntarakṣita
      • History: In June 1934, Sāṅkṛtyāyana found this manuscript in the monastery of Kun-de-ling (Lhasa).
